OVS (OpenvSwitch) Source Build CentOS7

Contents

  1. 1 Host OS Description
  2. 2 Preparing the RPM Build
  3. 3 Get Python 2.7 Installed
  4. 4 Building the RPMS
    1. 4.1 Create Required Build Directories
    2. 4.2 Download OpenvSwitch Tarball
    3. 4.3 Build the OpenvSwitch RPM
  5. 5 Install the OpenvSwitch RPM
  6. 6 Create the OpenvSwitch DB
  7. 7 Chkconfig OpenvSwitch
  8. 8 Verify OpenvSwitch Status
The guide here at Foswiki was my basic reference guide for the OpenvSwitch build on Oracle Linux 6 UEK kernel as well.  One significant difference on CentOS7 is that the additional steps to address the python version issue are not needed here on CentOS7 because CentOS7 already uses python27 by default.  Below are the detailed steps to build OpenvSwitch on CentOS7.

Host OS Description

The system that OpenvSwitch will be built on is described and characterized below.  Note that this is an Oracle Linux UEK kernel system.

[root@localhost ~]# uname -a
Linux localhost.localdomain 3.10.0-327.28.2.el7.x86_64 #1 SMP Wed Aug 3 11:11:39 UTC 2016 x86_64 x86_64 x86_64 GNU/Linux
[root@localhost ~]# cat /etc/redhat-release
CentOS Linux release 7.2.1511 (Core)
[root@localhost ~]# cat /etc/centos-release
CentOS Linux release 7.2.1511 (Core)
[root@localhost ~]#

[root@oracle67 SOURCES]#

Preparing the RPM Build

Be sure you have rpm-build installed.  On this CentOS7 system rpm-build is already installed as shown below but run this step to make sure it is already installed or use the 'rpm -qa | grep rpm-build' command.  In any case, be sure it is installed as shown below.

[root@localhost ~]# yum -y install rpm-build

Loaded plugins: fastestmirror, langpacks
base                                                                                                                                                                                        | 3.6 kB  00:00:00     
epel/x86_64/metalink                                                                                                                                                                        |  12 kB  00:00:00     
epel                                                                                                                                                                                        | 4.3 kB  00:00:00     
extras                                                                                                                                                                                      | 3.4 kB  00:00:00     
updates                                                                                                                                                                                     | 3.4 kB  00:00:00     
(1/2): epel/x86_64/updateinfo                                                                                                                                                               | 594 kB  00:00:00     
(2/2): epel/x86_64/primary_db                                                                                                                                                               | 4.3 MB  00:00:00     
Loading mirror speeds from cached hostfile
 * base: mirrors.gigenet.com
 * epel: lug.mtu.edu
 * extras: mirror.sesp.northwestern.edu
 * updates: mirrors.gigenet.com

Package rpm-build-4.11.3-17.el7.x86_64 already installed and latest version
Nothing to do

[root@localhost ~]#

Get Python 2.7 Installed

On CentOS7 python 2.7 is the default so it should already be installed.  Check it to be sure as shown below.

[root@localhost SOURCES]# yum -y install python27
Loaded plugins: fastestmirror, langpacks
Loading mirror speeds from cached hostfile
 * base: mirror.eboundhost.com
 * epel: lug.mtu.edu
 * extras: mirror.sesp.northwestern.edu
 * updates: mirror.team-cymru.org
No package python27 available.
Error: Nothing to do
[root@localhost SOURCES]#

[root@localhost ~]# python -V
Python 2.7.5
[root@localhost ~]#

Building the RPMS

Create Required Build Directories

[root@localhost ~]# mkdir -p ~/rpmbuild/SPECS
[root@localhost ~]# mkdir ~/rpmbuild/SOURCES

[root@localhost ~]# ls -lR
.:
total 4
-rw-------. 1 root root 1950 Aug 13 01:34 anaconda-ks.cfg
drwxr-xr-x. 4 root root   32 Aug 14 11:45 rpmbuild

./rpmbuild:
total 0
drwxr-xr-x. 2 root root 6 Aug 14 11:45 SOURCES
drwxr-xr-x. 2 root root 6 Aug 14 11:45 SPECS

./rpmbuild/SOURCES:
total 0

./rpmbuild/SPECS:
total 0
[root@localhost ~]#

Download OpenvSwitch Tarball

Next cd to the ~/rpmbuild/SOURCES directory and get the tarball as shown below.

[root@localhost ~]# cd ~/rpmbuild/SOURCES
[root@localhost SOURCES]# wget http://openvswitch.org/releases/openvswitch-2.5.0.tar.gz
--2016-08-14 11:48:46--  http://openvswitch.org/releases/openvswitch-2.5.0.tar.gz
Resolving openvswitch.org (openvswitch.org)... 69.56.251.103
Connecting to openvswitch.org (openvswitch.org)|69.56.251.103|:80... connected.
HTTP request sent, awaiting response... 200 OK
Length: 4603077 (4.4M) [application/x-gzip]
Saving to: ‘openvswitch-2.5.0.tar.gz’

100%[=========================================================================================================================================================================>] 4,603,077   5.33MB/s   in 0.8s  

2016-08-14 11:48:47 (5.33 MB/s) - ‘openvswitch-2.5.0.tar.gz’ saved [4603077/4603077]

[root@localhost SOURCES]# ls -lrt
total 4496
-rw-r--r--. 1 root root 4603077 Feb 27 12:40 openvswitch-2.5.0.tar.gz
[root@localhost SOURCES]#

We can then unpack the tar-ball so we can get the needed .spec files for use with rpmbuild as shown below.

[root@localhost SOURCES]# tar -zxvf openvswitch-2.5.0.tar.gz
[root@localhost SOURCES]# cp openvswitch-2.5.0/rhel/*.spec ~/rpmbuild/SPECS
[root@localhost SOURCES]#

Now navigate to the ~/rpmbuild/SPECS directory as shown below and verify that the spec files are there as shown below..

[root@localhost SOURCES]# cd ../SPECS/
[root@localhost SPECS]# ls -lrt
total 36
-rw-r--r--. 1 root root  1966 Aug 14 12:02 openvswitch-kmod-fedora.spec
-rw-r--r--. 1 root root 12749 Aug 14 12:02 openvswitch-fedora.spec
-rw-r--r--. 1 root root  2758 Aug 14 12:02 openvswitch-dkms.spec
-rw-r--r--. 1 root root  5689 Aug 14 12:02 openvswitch.spec
-rw-r--r--. 1 root root  2318 Aug 14 12:02 openvswitch-kmod-rhel6.spec
[root@localhost SPECS]# pwd
/root/rpmbuild/SPECS
[root@localhost SPECS]#

Build the OpenvSwitch RPM

Now build the openvswitch rpm as shown below. On my CentOS7 desktop system there was an unsatisfied dependency for openssl-devel so satisfy the dependency first as shown below.

[root@localhost SPECS]# rpmbuild -ba openvswitch.spec
error: Failed build dependencies:
    openssl-devel is needed by openvswitch-2.5.0-1.x86_64
[root@localhost SPECS]# yum install openssl-devel

 * epel: lug.mtu.edu
 * extras: mirrors.gigenet.com
 * updates: mirror.team-cymru.org

Now that the dependency is satisfied go ahead and try again to build the rpm from source as shown below.  The entire successful normal output of the build is shown.

                -e 's,[@]pkgdatadir[@],/usr/share/openvswitch,g' \
                -e 's,[@]sysconfdir[@],/etc,g' \
                -e 's,[@]bindir[@],/usr/bin,g' \
                -e 's,[@]sbindir[@],/usr/sbin,g' \
                -e 's,[@]abs_builddir[@],/root/rpmbuild/BUILD/openvswitch-2.5.0,g' \
                -e 's,[@]abs_top_srcdir[@],/root/rpmbuild/BUILD/openvswitch-2.5.0,g' \

                -e 's,[@]pkgdatadir[@],/usr/share/openvswitch,g' \
                -e 's,[@]sysconfdir[@],/etc,g' \
                -e 's,[@]bindir[@],/usr/bin,g' \
                -e 's,[@]sbindir[@],/usr/sbin,g' \

Create the OpenvSwitch DB

Now create the openvswitch db as shown below and then reboot.  Note you may need to create the openvswitch subdirectory under "/usr/local/etc" first (mkdir -p /usr/local/etc/openvswitch).

[root@localhost x86_64]# ovsdb-tool create /usr/local/etc/openvswitch/conf.db

Chkconfig OpenvSwitch

Verify that OpenvSwitch is set to start on boot as shonw below.

[root@localhost etc]# chkconfig --list openvswitch

Note: This output shows SysV services only and does not include native
      systemd services. SysV configuration data might be overridden by native
      systemd configuration.

      If you want to list systemd services use 'systemctl list-unit-files'.
      To see services enabled on particular target use
      'systemctl list-dependencies [target]'.

openvswitch        0:off    1:off    2:on    3:on    4:on    5:on    6:off
[root@localhost etc]#

Verify OpenvSwitch Status

After reboot, check that ovs-vsctl shows good status as shown below.
